            <div class="guide-text-wrapper"> 
             <div class="guide-head clearfix"> 
              <div class="guide-head-img-wrap"> 
               <img class="guide-head-img js-render" data-src="https://s3.graphiq.com/rx/img/default_mountain.svg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7"> 
              </div> 
              <div class="guide-head-right"> 
               <span class="stnd-sec-title-txt">Guide to Choosing Shopping Cart Software</span> 
              </div> 
             </div> 
             <div class="guide-contents">
              <div class="detail-card card-sec-card full-row"> 
               <div class="guide-header-wrap "> 
                <div class="data-block-body">
                 <div class="guide-chtml card-sec-el">
                  <div>
                   Shopping cart software is an e-commerce solution that allows consumers to make purchases online. Since many people prefer to do their shopping from the convenience of their homes, especially around the holidays, having an online presence is an essential way of doing business. Chances are that if you aren't selling products online, then your business is losing potential sales to competitors who do have an online store. An e-commerce shopping cart is therefore an indispensable tool for any merchant. Business owners who are not very knowledgeable in technological matters may think that setting up an online store is an expensive and time-consuming project, but with the modern software programs and services that are available, it is relatively easy to get things started quickly and cheaply. The key is choosing the right online shopping cart. However, with the plethora of shopping cart software solutions on the market, selecting the best one may seem like a daunting task. To facilitate the process, consider the following factors when weighing your options:
                   <br> 
                   <ul>
                    <li><b>Compatibility</b>: Before purchasing e-commerce shopping cart software, it is imperative to ensure that it is compatible with your web hosting. An ASP/MS SQL shopping cart, for instance, will not work on a Linux web server (and vice versa). You can also opt to switch hosts, but if you already have a website, this may not be a viable option for you.</li> 
                    <li><b>License Model</b>: Online shopping cart software will either be available for purchase (proprietary) or for free (open source). Open source software is available for free download and modification at no cost to the user, but this model can be very complicated for those who are unfamiliar with shopping cart software and computer programming. Proprietary software must be purchased for use. Although it is more expensive, this software is generally much easier to use than its open-source counterpart. You also will not have to configure the software or deal with any technical issues that may arise. </li> 
                    <li><b>Deployment Method</b>: You will also need to determine whether you want a hosted shopping cart or an client-server/on-premise shopping cart. A hosted solution functions similarly to any other web service you may sign-up for: you simply make an account and all the technical matters are taken care of for you. The only thing you need to do is access a web-based console, where you will be able to manage your online store. Hosted shopping carts are best for those who have little to no experience with e-commerce; however, this service will require monthly fees and may tie you down to one vendor. Another option is to download a shopping cart and install it on a web server through a license. Shopping cart software with a client-server deployment method offers greater flexibility and customization than hosted software, and it will also be cheaper in the long run. The downside is that it will require some basic technical knowledge to install it, and there may be a higher cost upfront. It should also be noted that client-server shopping carts tend to be open-source systems, which means you will have access to the source code of the software. Hosted shopping carts, on the other hand, tend to be proprietary programs that must be purchased for use. While these solutions usually do not include the source code as part of the license, some vendors will grant users access to the source code for an additional fee. </li>
                   </ul> 
                   <li><b>Features</b>: Consumers prefer user-friendly and aesthetically-pleasing online venues, so it is important for your software to have all the required features to make the layout visually engaging and easy to navigate. Some of the critical features all e-commerce stores should have include product reviews, order management/editing, coupon codes, shipping integration, and multiple payment processors, among others. However, there are many additional functions that may not be necessary; it just depends on your preferences and the type of features you want your online store to have. While several merchants may just need the basic functions, others may require all the attention-grabbing features of a big online website. </li> 
                   <br>Select and purchase the best shopping cart software according to your desired deployment method, features, license model, and database. Simply use the corresponding filters on the left side of the search results page to refine your search. You can also sort the various options by Smart Rating, price, license, and company name. Once you've narrowed it down to your top choices, compare the products side-by-side so you can better determine which shopping cart software program is best for your needs. 
                   <br> 
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>
             </div> 
            </div> 
           </div>

            <h2 class="stnd-sec-title-txt guide-cmp-title">Features</h2>
            <div class="guide-contents">
             <div class="detail-card card-sec-card full-row"> 
              <div class="guide-header-wrap "> 
               <div class="data-block-body"> 
                <div class="stnd-title" data-id="features"></div> 
                <div class="help-text">
                 Online shopping cart features allude to what is included in the software. Essentially, the features of a software package allow you to customize the look and feel of your online store. Good shopping cart software will allow you to monitor the activity in your e-store by showing you sales, search, and inventory reports, among other things. Many shopping carts will also have more advanced features, allowing you to create affiliate programs, customer registration, and other features to help your store grow. In the end, you should decide which features are needed for your own particular website. Some merchants may just need software with basic features, but others may require many additional features for a flourishing online website. Just make sure not to waste your money on functionality you don't need.
                </div>

           <div class="guide-sect-wrap" data-hash="22ed37eb40482baea3a3b46b4c57dfc51737ae7d">
            <h2 class="stnd-sec-title-txt guide-cmp-title">Customer Management Features</h2>
            <div class="guide-contents">
             <div class="detail-card card-sec-card full-row"> 
              <div class="guide-header-wrap "> 
               <div class="data-block-body"> 
                <div class="stnd-title" data-id="crm_feat"></div> 
                <div class="help-text">
                 Customer management functionality builds customer loyalty by helping to provide an exceptional online shopping experience. Customers may be able to create personal user accounts, track their orders, and see their order history directly from your online store. In addition to improving the overall user experience for your customers, these features can enable you to better understand your customers and ultimately improve your service.             <h2 class="stnd-sec-title-txt guide-cmp-title">Hosting and Security Features</h2>
            <div class="guide-contents">
             <div class="detail-card card-sec-card full-row"> 
              <div class="guide-header-wrap "> 
               <div class="data-block-body"> 
                <div class="stnd-title" data-id="host_sec_feat"></div> 
                <div class="help-text">
                 Hosting and security functionality helps to ensure your data and customer information stay secure. Hosting is the backbone of all e-commerce activities, so it is imperative to choose a shopping cart software solution that boasts the best and most secure service with multiple data centers and points of access. Security is another necessity--it is a chief concern for online shoppers, so it's crucial to make sure that the shopping cart you use offers standard security features. These should include suspicious activity tracking, SSL secure checkouts that encrypt customers' payment information, as well as data backup and restoration to protect your business records.
                </div> 
                <div class="help-viz-wrapper">
                 <div class="coviz-barAppData coviz-wrap" data-cotype="barAppData" data-cobase="bar" data-co-needs-update="1" data-hash="2B1PhlGMJzv5MA9r"></div>
                 <div class="coviz-caption">
                  The chart above displays the percentage breakdown of 
                  <i>hosting and security features</i> across all Shopping Cart on SoftwareInsider.
                 </div>
                </div> 
                <div class="app-data-desc-wrap">
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="8">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Antivirus
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Your website will be scanned daily for thousands of hacker vulnerabilities.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="10">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Daily Backup
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software automatically backups your data every day, just in case you delete or overwrite any file you may need to restore.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="7">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Data Encryption
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">All the data on your website will be encrypted. Encryption is the process of scrambling a message to ensure data secrecy and security. The message is encoded using an electronic key, which makes it unintelligible to anyone except to the holders of the other half of the key.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="13">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Data Indexing
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software indexes all dynamic data on your website.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="17">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Database Caching
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software caches a certain percentage of your website database to improve performance.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="6">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Dedicated SSL
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   Add a dedicated secure sockets layer (SSL) certificate to your website. It offers privacy, authentication, and security. A dedicated SSL certificate will allow you and your customers to conduct Internet transactions referencing a secure URL at your own domain name. Adding an SSL certificate to your website lets your customers know that their personal information is safe and that transactions are secure in two ways. First, an "https" prefix will display in their address bar to identify your site as protected. Secondly, a certificate will be issued to encrypt data transfers like credit card numbers, and to identify your website as the same one on file with the Certificate Authority.
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="3">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Firewall Protection
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">A firewall will be installed to protect all access points.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="11">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   FTP Access
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Easily upload and manage your files using FTP.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="9">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Injection Monitoring
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software prevents SQL injections from happening on the servers.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="12">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   IP Blocking
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Block a specific Internet Protocol (IP) address that a customer used when placing an order. This will be useful when you suspect fraudulent activity and want to block the source of potentially fraudulent orders.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="14">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   IPV6 Support
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software can support the latest revision of the Internet Protocol (IP).</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="1">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   PCI Compliance
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   The software vendor is certified and compliant with the strict security standards outlined by the Payment Card Industry (PCI). These standards have been endorsed by every major credit card company and adopted as the standard security method when handling credit cards over the Internet. This enables you to accept Visa, MasterCard, and other major credit cards as payment.
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="15">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Performance Benchmarking
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software consistently performs benchmarks on your database and website to improve performance.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="18">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Redundant DNS
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Create multiple domain names. If your main site goes down, this helps to ensure that customers will still be able to find and use your website.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="16">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Search Caching
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software caches all search results every 24 hours to improve performance.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="5">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Shared SSL
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Add a shared SSL certificate to your website. A secure socket layer (SSL) will provide privacy, authentication, and security. With a shared SSL certificate, someone else usually has the certificate and will agree to add you to the certificate or to let you use it for a small fee.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="4">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Suspicious Activity Tracking
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">The software will alert you of any suspicious activity on your website.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div> 
               </div> 
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="guide-sect-wrap" data-hash="5ffff564f78f5078ba5577017271dd0e0f3a9e86">
            <h2 class="stnd-sec-title-txt guide-cmp-title">Reporting and Analysis</h2>
            <div class="guide-contents">
             <div class="detail-card card-sec-card full-row"> 
              <div class="guide-header-wrap "> 
               <div class="data-block-body"> 
                <div class="stnd-title" data-id="report"></div> 
                <div class="help-text">
                 Reporting and analysis functionality provides better insight to customer activity and behavior. These features can help you track specific site statistics such as individual visits and referrals. You can even add conversion tracking with Google Analytics to determine your store’s marketing and ROI statistics. Certain reporting features also allow you to review individual product performance such as top selling items, monthly and daily product activity, and gift-certificate sales. Additionally, you can generate reports on inventory results to keep your store well stocked with your top-selling items.
                </div> 
                <div class="help-viz-wrapper">
                 <div class="coviz-barAppData coviz-wrap" data-cotype="barAppData" data-cobase="bar" data-co-needs-update="1" data-hash="QYusBrGtZTHFpLiP"></div>
                 <div class="coviz-caption">
                  The chart above displays the percentage breakdown of 
                  <i>reporting and analysis</i> across all Shopping Cart on SoftwareInsider.
                 </div>
                </div> 
                <div class="app-data-desc-wrap">
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="6">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Balance Sheets
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">View the complete balance sheet with charts for year-round performance.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="7">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Behavior Analytics
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Track incoming traffic and mouse movements to gather certain information about customer activity and behavior, such as the duration and destination of a particular visit.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="3">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Hosting Usage Reports
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">View your hosting account's bandwidth usage.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="11">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Inventory Reports
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Track prices, profitability, and transactions affecting the value of products in inventory. You can also see the current status and count of items in inventory.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="10">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Keyword Rank Tracking
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Track your rank in search engine results for certain keywords and phrases over time.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="1">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Product Performance Reports
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Better understand how products are selling in different categories. You can see the sales by product for a specific date, including total units sold and value of the items sold.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="5">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Profit/Loss Reports
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Track, monitor, and visualize your profits and losses over a certain period of time.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="2">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Sales Summary Reports
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">See a summary of all orders within a specified time period. The report will usually include total net and gross sales, number of orders placed, average orders per day, and average amount per order. It also typically highlights the best-selling and worst-selling products.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="4">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Storage Usage Reports
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">View your hosting account's disk space usage.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="8">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Traffic Analytics
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Track site statistics such as individual visits and referrals, page views, bounce rate, and much more.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <div class="app-data-guide" data-key="9">
                  <div class="app-data-val">
                   Traffic ROI Tracking
                  </div>
                  <div class="app-data-desc">
                   <span class="snippet">Analyze incoming traffic and conversion levels, and keep track of several campaigns simultaneously. You will be able to measure visitor engagement on your website more effectively and better understand the conversion trends.</span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div> 
               </div> 
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="guide-sect-wrap" data-hash="53eee1e0fbd12e0b7a346ee36085c73cee9a5020">

           <div class="guide-sect-wrap" data-hash="710275fc36faf0c59bdf3ab1bbc93a12c5353057">
            <h2 class="stnd-sec-title-txt guide-cmp-title">What to Watch for When Choosing Shopping Cart Software</h2>
            <div class="guide-contents">
             <div class="detail-card card-sec-card full-row"> 
              <div class="guide-header-wrap "> 
               <div class="data-block-body">
                <div class="guide-chtml card-sec-el">
                 <div>
                  <b>Overspending</b> 
                  <br>Despite the various features that e-commerce shopping cart software can boast, refrain from going overboard and dropping a lot of cash on functionality you don't need. You can always upgrade to more extensive software in the future if your needs change. 
                  <br> 
                  <br>
                  <b>Customer Support</b> 
                  <br>Before deciding on a software package, ensure the company provides adequate technical support. You will probably require assistance for either installing, setting up, configuring, or customizing the cart to fit your website. Also, bugs and security issues would need to be addressed immediately. It is therefore imperative to ensure that technical support is readily available—a small delay can lead to a significant amount of lost sales and revenues. 
                  <br>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div> 
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
